  4→Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the \"License\");\n     5→you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.\n     6→You may obtain a copy of the License at\n \"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1\"\n    24→\t\"k8s.io/pod-security-admission/api\"\n    25→)\n    26→\n    27→type Check struct {\n    28→\t// ID is the unique ID of the check.\n    29→\tID CheckID\n    30→\t// Level is the policy level this check belongs to.\n    31→\t// Must be Baseline or Restricted.\n    32→\t// Baseline checks are evaluated for baseline and restricted namespaces.\n    33→\t// Restricted checks are only evaluated for restricted namespaces.\n    34→\tLevel api.Level\n    35→\t// Versions contains one or more revisions of the check that apply to different versions.\n    36→\t// If the check is not yet assigned to a version, this must be a single-item list with a MinimumVersion of \"\".\n    37→\t// Otherwise, MinimumVersion of items must represent strictly increasing versions.\n    38→\tVersions []VersionedCheck\n    39→}\n    40→\n    41→type VersionedCheck struct {\n    42→\t// MinimumVersion is the first policy version this check applies to.\n    43→\t// If unset, this check is not yet assigned to a policy version.\n    44→\t// If set, must not be \"latest\".\n    45→\tMinimumVersion api.Version\n    46→\t// CheckPod determines if the pod is allowed.\n    47→\tCheckPod CheckPodFn\n    48→\t// OverrideCheckIDs is an optional list of checks that should be skipped when this check is run.\n    49→\t// Overrides may only be set on restricted checks, and may only override baseline checks.\n    50→\tOverrideCheckIDs []CheckID\n    51→}\n    52→\n    53→type CheckPodFn func(*metav1.ObjectMeta, *corev1.PodSpec) CheckResult\n    54→\n    55→type CheckID string\n    56→\n    57→// CheckResult contains the result of checking a pod and indicates whether the pod is allowed,\n    58→// and if not, why it was forbidden.\n    59→//\n    60→// Example output for (false, \"host ports\", \"8080, 9090\"):\n    61→//\n    62→//\tWhen checking all pods in a namespace:\n    63→//\t  disallowed by policy \"baseline\": host ports, privileged containers, non-default capabilities\n    64→//\tWhen checking an individual pod:\n    65→//\t  disallowed by policy \"baseline\": host ports (8080, 9090), privileged containers, non-default capabilities (CAP_NET_RAW)\n    66→type CheckResult struct {\n    67→\t// Allowed indicates if the check allowed the pod.\n    68→\tAllowed bool\n    69→\t// ForbiddenReason must be set if (staging/src/k8s.io/pod-security-admission/policy/):\\nThe primary validation logic is located in the pod-security-admission policy package, which implements security policy checks at both baseline and restricted levels:\\n\\n1. **runAsNonRoot Enforcement** (check_runAsNonRoot.go): The CheckRunAsNonRoot() function returns a restricted level check that enforces runAsNonRoot=true. The runAsNonRoot_1_0() validator checks that containers either explicitly set runAsNonRoot=true or inherit it from pod-level security context, using visitContainers() to traverse all container types.\\n\\n2. **Privileged Container Check** (check_privileged.go): The CheckPrivileged() function returns a baseline level check that forbids privileged=true. The privileged_1_0() validator examines container.SecurityContext.Privileged field and rejects any container with Privileged=true.\\n\\n3. **Capabilities Validation** spans two files:\\n   - check_capabilities_baseline.go: CheckCapabilitiesBaseline() enforces baseline constraints, allowing only default capabilities like AUDIT_WRITE, CHOWN, DAC_OVERRIDE, FOWNER, FSETID, KILL, MKNOD, NET_BIND_SERVICE, SETFCAP, SETGID, SETPCAP, SETUID, and SYS_CHROOT. The capabilitiesBaseline_1_0() function checks SecurityContext.Capabilities.Add against an allowed set.\\n   - check_capabilities_restricted.go: CheckCapabilitiesRestricted() enforces restricted level constraints requiring ALL capabilities to be dropped and allowing only NET_BIND_SERVICE to be added. The capabilitiesRestricted_1_22() function checks both Capabilities.Drop (must include \\\"ALL\\\") and Capabilities.Add (must only contain \\\"NET_BIND_SERVICE\\\").\\n\\n4. **Seccomp Profile
